< review>
I am the HERS Rater for AirWorks Solutions. I inspect their systems and perform the energy efficiency tests required by the State of California. There are several tests which measure how efficient a system is functioning, including duct leakage, airflow rate and refrigerant levels. I am an independent third party inspector with no affiliation with the company.

Their systems routinely pass inspection. Duct systems are sealed to prevent leakage into unconditioned space (ie. attics and wall cavities), return duct sizing is appropriately sized and air conditioners always have the right amount of charge.

Many contractors don't seal existing duct systems when just a furnace or AC is replaced. THIS IS REQUIRED! This step is the primary reason why systems fail to pass inspection. AirWorks Solutions understands this and always seals their systems.

This is why I recommend AirWorks Solutions, they follow the building code and always adhere to the highest standards of installation quality and ethical business practices.</review>

FIRST REVIEW:

We are now going to have another company check things out and provide a second opinion.  AirWorks Solutions didn't get our air to work - their solution was a total failure. Dr. Takher identified a huge undiagnosed cavity and extracted an ailing/cracked tooth that should have removed years ago. I have to give special thanks and appreciation to Tyra, the best Dental Hygienist anywhere she has been cleaning my teeth for years and treated and cured me of minor gum disease that could have developed into a severe medical problem.  I can never be reassigned from Tyra's care!  In short, Pena Adobe Dental Care is world class, to prove that I drive from the Bay Area to receive my dental care from this excellent, young, knowledgeable, caring and cutting edge team.  Thank you. Jim</review>

<Pictures>None</Pictures>< review>
A few years ago I took my car to get smogged here. I had just replaced the battery (which will autofail the smog test) and took it here to get smogged without realizing the situation. Before the test started I told the mechanic what had happened. He knew that it would fail the test, and still completed it anyways. I don't really understand this logic, as he could've charged me a 10 dollar advice fee or something and I would've come back to this shop, where they would've gotten the same amount of money. I have no doubt they are capable mechanics, but since that experience I can not recommend them as I can not trust them. Seem to focus on making an immediate dollar at all costs over keeping a customer due to proximity to Isla Vista.< /review>

<rate>4</rate>< review>
We came here for late night food after a drag show nearby. Service was top notch. Even though they were busy, we still found seating for our group.

We ordered nachos and the grilled cheese. The nachos came out on a sheet tray with an entire pound of melted cheese goodness. The sauce is quite spicy though.

The grilled cheese.... out of this world. Three sandwich halves and loaded with cheese. That may be the best grilled cheese ever.</review>

< Review>
Beware there is a bartender here ripping people off!  Avoid the bartender with the handle bar mustache. This guy tried to rip me off on 2 separate occasions.

I love the hot chicken sandwich at this place because it's amazing. I frequent this spot pretty regularly as the food is good. I usually have no issues at at with every other staff member.

I'll start with last night. My partner and I ordered 2 chicken sandwiches and 2 vodka lemonades on our way home from running errands. The bartender put in our order wrong and seemed unapologetic as he didn't even say something like "hey my bad" which would've been cool. So we get our bill in a shot glass as we were sitting at the bar. Our bill was about 42.00. I paid 25.00 cash and my partner put his card down for the remaining balance and tip.

He grabbed the glass and said "what are we doing guys?" You want the money towards the bill and rest on the card? We said "yes". He came back with a receipt for 16.62 and my partner signed it and tipped him. We get home and an alert pops up that he charged the entire bill to his card and pocketed my cash.

Another incident happens about 3 months ago when I gave him 60.00 on a 42 dollar tab. He asked me if I wanted change and I said "Yes, please" he not only didn't come back but went and took a break. When he returned he never came back to me so I asked someone else behind the bar if I could get my change? The handlebar mustache guy rolls his eyes and then gives me my change.

How many other people is this guy doing this to and why is this allowed to take place? This guy needs to be fired and should never be allowed around the cash register. Buyer beware and order from anyone else.</Review>

< user_name>
N√´co Rey</user_name>
< Rate>
5<//Rate>
< text>
The owner is always friendly, funny, and attractive in the same uniform as everybody else: black shirt, and jeans of some sort.

Hand selected the menu items, based off of his own likes.

The drinks are crafted, and not thrown together with extra rubbing alcohol, like every other bar.

It's technically a restaurant, technically a bar, and technically gay, but not really.

The music is eclectic, and a Droid video of India plays on the screen whenever there isn't a muted, classic movie on.

I personally love the vegan sandwich called the "Conscientious Objector, which has the flavor of pulled pork, with the texture of meatloaf. Delish!

Overall, it's the best bar to ever open up on Arenas, and I hope it's success continues!</text>
